16:49:25.844 [gremlin-server-worker-1] WARN  o.a.t.g.s.h.OpExecutorHandler - Procedure call cannot take an aggregating function as argument, please add a 'WITH' to your statement.

    MATCH (n:Person) WITH collect(n.name) AS names CALL proc(names) YIELD value RETURN value (line 2, column 1 (offset: 10))
org.opencypher.v9_0.util.SyntaxException: Procedure call cannot take an aggregating function as argument, please add a 'WITH' to your statement.
